  <script>
    const reveals = document.querySelectorAll('.reveal');
    const io = new IntersectionObserver(entries => {
      entries.forEach((e,i) => {
        if (e.isIntersecting) { setTimeout(() => e.target.classList.add('visible'), i * 60); io.unobserve(e.target); }
      });
    }, { threshold:0.08 });
    reveals.forEach(el => io.observe(el));

    document.querySelectorAll('.stat-num[data-target]').forEach(el => {
      const target = parseFloat(el.dataset.target);
      const prefix = el.dataset.prefix || '';
      const isFloat = target % 1 !== 0;
      const dur = 1800;
      const obs = new IntersectionObserver(entries => {
        if (entries[0].isIntersecting) {
          const t0 = performance.now();
          const tick = now => {
            const prog = Math.min((now - t0) / dur, 1);
            const ease = 1 - Math.pow(1 - prog, 3);
            const val  = target * ease;
            if (target >= 10000) { el.textContent = prefix + Math.floor(val).toLocaleString('en-IN'); }
            else if (isFloat)    { el.textContent = prefix + val.toFixed(1); }
            else                 { el.textContent = prefix + Math.floor(val).toLocaleString('en-IN'); }
            if (prog < 1) requestAnimationFrame(tick);
          };
          requestAnimationFrame(tick);
          obs.disconnect();
        }
      });
      obs.observe(el);
    });

    function filterTable(q) {
      document.querySelectorAll('#tableBody tr').forEach(row => {
        row.style.display = row.textContent.toLowerCase().includes(q.toLowerCase()) ? '' : 'none';
      });
    }

    let sortDir = {};
    function sortTable(col) {
      const tbody = document.getElementById('tableBody');
      const rows  = Array.from(tbody.querySelectorAll('tr'));
      sortDir[col] = !sortDir[col];
      rows.sort((a, b) => {
        const ta = a.cells[col].textContent.trim();
        const tb = b.cells[col].textContent.trim();
        const na = parseFloat(ta.replace(/[^0-9.]/g,''));
        const nb = parseFloat(tb.replace(/[^0-9.]/g,''));
        if (!isNaN(na) && !isNaN(nb)) return sortDir[col] ? na-nb : nb-na;
        return sortDir[col] ? ta.localeCompare(tb) : tb.localeCompare(ta);
      });
      rows.forEach(r => tbody.appendChild(r));
    }

    function exportReport() {
      const rows  = document.querySelectorAll('#eventsTable tr');
      const lines = [];
      rows.forEach(r => {
        const cells = Array.from(r.querySelectorAll('th,td')).slice(0,8);
        lines.push(cells.map(c => '"' + c.textContent.trim().replace(/"/g,'""') + '"').join(','));
      });
      const blob = new Blob([lines.join('\n')], {type:'text/csv'});
      const a = document.createElement('a');
      a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob); a.download = 'eventra-report.csv'; a.click();
    }

    let altMode = false;
    function toggleChartType() {
      altMode = !altMode;
      document.querySelectorAll('#barChart .bar').forEach(b => {
        const cur = parseInt(b.style.height || 0);
        b.style.height = (altMode ? Math.max(20, cur - 15) : cur) + '%';
      });
    }
  </script>

</body>
</html>

    *, *::before, *::after { box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0; padding: 0; }

<!-- ONLY JS PART UPDATED (your HTML + CSS remain same) -->
<script>
  let selectedEmoji = '🎨';

  window.onload = updatePreview;

  function updatePreview() {
    const title  = document.getElementById('eventTitle').value || 'Your event title will appear here…';
    const cat    = document.getElementById('eventCat').value || 'Category';
    const date   = document.getElementById('eventDate').value;
    const time   = document.getElementById('eventTime').value;
    const venue  = document.getElementById('eventVenue').value || 'Venue / Location';
    const price  = document.getElementById('tier1Price')?.value;

    document.getElementById('previewTitle').textContent = title;
    document.getElementById('previewTag').textContent = cat;

    // Only show emoji if no image
    const banner = document.getElementById('previewBanner');
    if (!banner.style.backgroundImage) {
      banner.textContent = selectedEmoji;
    }

    document.getElementById('previewDate').textContent = date
      ? '📅 ' + new Date(date).toLocaleDateString('en-IN', {
          day: 'numeric', month: 'short', year: 'numeric'
        }) + (time ? ', ' + time : '')
      : '📅 Date & Time';

    document.getElementById('previewVenue').textContent = '📍 ' + venue;

    document.getElementById('previewPrice').textContent =
      price && !isNaN(price)
        ? '₹' + Number(price).toLocaleString('en-IN')
        : 'Free';
  }

  function updateChar(inputId, countId, max) {
    const len = document.getElementById(inputId).value.length;
    document.getElementById(countId).textContent = len + '/' + max;
  }

  function selectEmoji(el, emoji) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.emoji-opt').forEach(e => e.style.background = '');
    el.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg,rgba(253,232,240,.6),rgba(232,234,255,.6))';
    selectedEmoji = emoji;

    // reset image if emoji selected
    const banner = document.getElementById('previewBanner');
    banner.style.backgroundImage = '';
    banner.textContent = emoji;

    updatePreview();
  }

  const tags = [];
  function addTag(e) {
    if (e.key === 'Enter') {
      e.preventDefault();
      const val = e.target.value.trim();
      if (val && !tags.includes(val)) {
        tags.push(val);
        const chip = document.createElement('div');
        chip.className = 'tag-chip';
        chip.innerHTML = val + `<button onclick="removeTag(this,'${val}')">✕</button>`;
        document.getElementById('tagsWrap').insertBefore(chip, e.target);
      }
      e.target.value = '';
    }
  }

  function removeTag(btn, val) {
    const index = tags.indexOf(val);
    if (index > -1) tags.splice(index, 1);
    btn.parentElement.remove();
  }

  const tierColors = [
    'linear-gradient(135deg,#a070d0,#c9b8f0)',
    'linear-gradient(135deg,#50b8d8,#aaecdc)',
    'linear-gradient(135deg,#f9c784,#f4a7b9)'
  ];

  let tierCount = 1;

  function addTier() {
    tierCount++;
    const t = document.createElement('div');
    t.className = 'tier-card';
    t.innerHTML = `
      <div class="tier-color" style="background:${tierColors[(tierCount-1)%tierColors.length]};"></div>
      <div class="tier-fields">
        <input type="text" placeholder="Tier name" style="flex:2;"/>
        <input type="number" placeholder="Price (₹)" style="flex:1;"/>
        <input type="number" placeholder="Qty" style="flex:1;"/>
      </div>
      <button class="tier-remove" onclick="removeTier(this)">✕</button>`;
    document.getElementById('tierList').appendChild(t);
  }

  function removeTier(btn) {
    const tiers = document.querySelectorAll('.tier-card');
    if (tiers.length > 1) btn.closest('.tier-card').remove();
  }

  function handleUpload(e) {
    const preview = document.getElementById('uploadPreview');
    preview.style.display = 'flex';

    [...e.target.files].forEach(file => {
      const reader = new FileReader();
      reader.onload = ev => {
        const img = document.createElement('img');
        img.src = ev.target.result;
        img.className = 'preview-img';
        preview.appendChild(img);

        const banner = document.getElementById('previewBanner');
        banner.style.backgroundImage = `url(${ev.target.result})`;
        banner.style.backgroundSize = 'cover';
        banner.style.backgroundPosition = 'center';
        banner.textContent = '';
      };
      reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    });
  }

  function goStep(n, el) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.step-item').forEach((s,i) => {
      s.classList.remove('active','done');
      if (i + 1 < n) s.classList.add('done');
    });
    el.classList.add('active');
    document.getElementById('section' + n).scrollIntoView({ behavior:'smooth' });
  }

  function showToast(icon, title, msg) {
    document.getElementById('toastIcon').textContent = icon;
    document.getElementById('toastTitle').textContent = title;
    document.getElementById('toastMsg').textContent = msg;

    const t = document.getElementById('toast');
    t.classList.add('show');
    setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), 3500);
  }

  function submitEvent() {
    const title = document.getElementById('eventTitle').value.trim();
    const date = document.getElementById('eventDate').value;
    const time = document.getElementById('eventTime').value;
    const venue = document.getElementById('eventVenue').value.trim();

    if (!title || !date || !time || !venue) {
      showToast('⚠️','Missing Info','Please fill all required fields.');
      return;
    }

    showToast('🎉','Event Published!','Your event is now live and visible to everyone.');
    setTimeout(() => location.href='event-details.html', 2000);
  }

  function saveDraft() {
    showToast('💾','Draft Saved','Your event has been saved.');
  }
</script>
</body>
</html>

  <script>
    const reveals = document.querySelectorAll('.reveal');
    const io = new IntersectionObserver(entries => {
      entries.forEach((e, i) => {
        if (e.isIntersecting) {
          setTimeout(() => e.target.classList.add('visible'), i * 80);
          io.unobserve(e.target);
        }
      });
    }, { threshold: 0.12 });
    reveals.forEach(el => io.observe(el));

    document.querySelectorAll('.stat-num').forEach(el => {
      const text = el.textContent;
      const num = parseFloat(text.replace(/[^0-9.]/g,''));
      const suffix = text.replace(/[0-9.]/g,'');
      let start = 0;
      const dur = 1800;
      const step = ts => {
        if (!start) start = ts;
        const prog = Math.min((ts - start) / dur, 1);
        el.textContent = (num * prog).toFixed(num % 1 ? 1 : 0) + suffix;
        if (prog < 1) requestAnimationFrame(step);
      };
      const obs = new IntersectionObserver(entries => {
        if (entries[0].isIntersecting) {
          requestAnimationFrame(step);
          obs.disconnect();
        }
      });
      obs.observe(el);
    });
  </script>
</body>
</html>

  <script>
    let basePrice = 499, ticketLabel = 'General Admission', qty = 1, addonTotal = 0;
    const PLATFORM_FEE = 25;
    let currentStep = 1;

    function setStep(n) {
      for (let i = 1; i <= 4; i++) {
        const s = document.getElementById('step' + i);
        if (!s) continue;
        s.classList.remove('active', 'done');
        if (i < n)   s.classList.add('done');
        if (i === n) s.classList.add('active');
      }
      for (let i = 1; i <= 3; i++) {
        const l = document.getElementById('line' + i);
        if (!l) continue;
        if (i < n) l.classList.add('done');
        else       l.classList.remove('done');
      }
    }

    function showStep(n) {
      currentStep = n;
      document.getElementById('cardStep1').style.display  = n === 1 ? 'block' : 'none';
      document.getElementById('cardStep2').style.display  = n === 2 ? 'block' : 'none';
      document.getElementById('cardStep3').style.display  = n === 3 ? 'block' : 'none';
      document.getElementById('submitWrap').style.display = n === 3 ? 'block' : 'none';
      setStep(n);
      window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
    }

    function validateStep1() {
      const fname = document.getElementById('firstName').value.trim();
      const email = document.getElementById('emailInput').value.trim();
      const phone = document.getElementById('phoneInput').value.trim();
      if (!fname) { showToast('⚠️','Missing Name','Please enter your first name.'); document.getElementById('firstName').focus(); return false; }
      if (!email || !/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(email)) { showToast('⚠️','Invalid Email','Please enter a valid email address.'); document.getElementById('emailInput').focus(); return false; }
      if (!phone) { showToast('⚠️','Missing Phone','Please enter your phone number.'); document.getElementById('phoneInput').focus(); return false; }
      return true;
    }

    function goToStep(n) {
      if (n === currentStep) return;
      // Going backwards — always free
      if (n < currentStep) { showStep(n); return; }
      // Going forwards — must pass step 1 validation
      if (!validateStep1()) return;
      // Step 4 = submit
      if (n === 4) { submitRegistration(); return; }
      showStep(n);
    }

    function nextStep() {
      if (currentStep === 1 && !validateStep1()) return;
      if (currentStep < 3) showStep(currentStep + 1);
    }

    function prevStep() {
      if (currentStep > 1) showStep(currentStep - 1);
    }

    function calcTotal() {
      const sub   = basePrice * qty + addonTotal;
      const gst   = Math.round((sub + PLATFORM_FEE) * 0.18);
      const total = sub + PLATFORM_FEE + gst;
      document.getElementById('ticketLabel').textContent    = ticketLabel + ' × ' + qty;
      document.getElementById('ticketSubtotal').textContent = '₹' + (basePrice * qty).toLocaleString('en-IN');
      document.getElementById('gstAmt').textContent         = '₹' + gst.toLocaleString('en-IN');
      document.getElementById('grandTotal').textContent     = '₹' + total.toLocaleString('en-IN');
      document.getElementById('paidAmt').textContent        = '₹' + total.toLocaleString('en-IN');
      if (addonTotal > 0) {
        document.getElementById('addonRow').style.display = 'flex';
        document.getElementById('addonTotal').textContent = '₹' + addonTotal.toLocaleString('en-IN');
      } else {
        document.getElementById('addonRow').style.display = 'none';
      }
    }

    function selectTicket(el, price, label) {
      document.querySelectorAll('.ticket-opt').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('selected'));
      el.classList.add('selected');
      basePrice = price; ticketLabel = label;
      calcTotal();
    }

    function changeQty(d) {
      qty = Math.max(1, Math.min(10, qty + d));
      document.getElementById('qtyNum').textContent = qty;
      calcTotal();
    }

    function toggleAddon(el, price) {
      el.classList.toggle('checked');
      addonTotal += el.classList.contains('checked') ? price : -price;
      calcTotal();
    }

    function selectPay(el) {
      document.querySelectorAll('.pay-opt').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
      el.classList.add('active');
    }

    function toggleCheck(row) {
      row.querySelector('.custom-check').classList.toggle('checked');
    }

    function validateName(inp) {
      inp.classList.toggle('input-valid',   inp.value.trim().length >= 2);
      inp.classList.toggle('input-invalid', inp.value.trim().length > 0 && inp.value.trim().length < 2);
    }
    function validateEmail(inp) {
      const ok  = /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(inp.value);
      const msg = document.getElementById('emailMsg');
      inp.classList.toggle('input-valid',   ok);
      inp.classList.toggle('input-invalid', inp.value.length > 0 && !ok);
      msg.textContent = inp.value.length > 0 ? (ok ? '✓ Looks good!' : 'Please enter a valid email.') : '';
      msg.className   = 'field-msg ' + (ok ? 'ok' : 'err');
    }
    function validatePhone(inp) {
      const ok  = /^[\+\d\s\-]{8,15}$/.test(inp.value);
      const msg = document.getElementById('phoneMsg');
      inp.classList.toggle('input-valid',   ok);
      inp.classList.toggle('input-invalid', inp.value.length > 0 && !ok);
      msg.textContent = inp.value.length > 0 ? (ok ? '✓ Valid number' : 'Enter a valid phone number.') : '';
      msg.className   = 'field-msg ' + (ok ? 'ok' : 'err');
    }

    function formatCard(inp) {
      let v = inp.value.replace(/\D/g,'').substring(0,16);
      inp.value = v.replace(/(.{4})/g,'$1  ').trim();
    }
    function formatExpiry(inp) {
      let v = inp.value.replace(/\D/g,'');
      if (v.length >= 2) v = v.substring(0,2) + ' / ' + v.substring(2,4);
      inp.value = v;
    }

    function showToast(icon, title, msg) {
      document.getElementById('toastIcon').textContent  = icon;
      document.getElementById('toastTitle').textContent = title;
      document.getElementById('toastMsg').textContent   = msg;
      const t = document.getElementById('toast');
      t.classList.add('show');
      setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), 3500);
    }

    function submitRegistration() {
      const bid = 'EVT-2025-' + Math.floor(1000 + Math.random() * 9000);
      document.getElementById('bookingId').textContent = bid;
      setStep(4);
      document.getElementById('successScreen').classList.add('show');
      document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
    }

    calcTotal();
    showStep(1);
  </script>

</body>
</html>


      5.event-details.html

  <style>
    *, *::before, *::after { box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0; padding: 0; }

      --text-dark:    #3a2a3e;
      --text-mid:     #7a6080;

      --radius:       20px;
      --nav-h:        72px;
    }

    html { scroll-behavior: smooth; }

    body {
      font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
      background: linear-gradient(135deg, #fde8f0 0%, #fef3e2 30%, #e8eaff 65%, #e0f7f4 100%);
      min-height: 100vh;
      color: var(--text-dark);
      overflow-x: hidden;
    }

    .blob { position:fixed; border-radius:50%; filter:blur(80px); opacity:.4; pointer-events:none; z-index:0; }

  <script>
    const reveals = document.querySelectorAll('.reveal');
    const io = new IntersectionObserver(entries => {
      entries.forEach(e => {
        if (e.isIntersecting) { e.target.classList.add('visible'); io.unobserve(e.target); }
      });
    }, { threshold: 0.1 });
    reveals.forEach(el => io.observe(el));

    let qty = 1;
    const price = 499;
    function changeQty(delta) {
      qty = Math.max(1, Math.min(10, qty + delta));
      document.getElementById('qtyNum').textContent = qty;
      document.getElementById('totalPrice').textContent = '₹' + (qty * price).toLocaleString('en-IN');
    }

    function toggleWish(btn) {
      const saved = btn.textContent.includes('❤️');
      btn.textContent = saved ? '🤍 Save' : '❤️ Saved';
    }

    function copyLink() {
      navigator.clipboard.writeText(window.location.href).then(() => {
        alert('Link copied to clipboard!');
      });
    }

    function shareEvent() {
      if (navigator.share) {
        navigator.share({ title: 'UI / UX Masterclass 2025', url: window.location.href });
      } else {
        copyLink();
      }
    }
  </script>

  <script>
    const tabs = ['dashboard','events','users','registrations','revenue','reviews','reports','settings','logs'];
    const tabTitles = { dashboard:'Dashboard', events:'Event Management', users:'User Management', registrations:'Registrations', revenue:'Revenue', reviews:'Review Moderation', reports:'Reports', settings:'Settings', logs:'Audit Logs' };

    function showTab(name) {
      tabs.forEach(t => { const el = document.getElementById('tab-'+t); if(el) el.style.display='none'; });
      const target = document.getElementById('tab-'+name);
      if(target) { target.style.display='block'; }
      document.getElementById('navTitle').textContent = tabTitles[name] || name;
      document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-nav a').forEach(a => {
        a.classList.remove('active');
        if(a.getAttribute('onclick') && a.getAttribute('onclick').includes("'"+name+"'")) a.classList.add('active');
      });
      window.scrollTo({top:0,behavior:'smooth'});
      setTimeout(() => document.querySelectorAll('.reveal').forEach(el => el.classList.add('visible')), 100);
      animateCounters();
    }

    const io = new IntersectionObserver(entries => { entries.forEach(e => { if(e.isIntersecting){ e.target.classList.add('visible'); io.unobserve(e.target); } }); }, {threshold:0.08});
    document.querySelectorAll('.reveal').forEach(el => io.observe(el));

    function animateCounters() {
      document.querySelectorAll('.stat-num[data-target]').forEach(el => {
        delete el.dataset.animated;
        const target = parseFloat(el.dataset.target);
        const prefix = el.dataset.prefix || '';
        const isFloat = target % 1 !== 0;
        const dur = 1600; const t0 = performance.now();
        const tick = now => {
          const prog = Math.min((now-t0)/dur,1);
          const ease = 1 - Math.pow(1-prog,3);
          const val = target * ease;
          if(target>=10000) el.textContent = prefix + Math.floor(val).toLocaleString('en-IN');
          else if(isFloat)  el.textContent = prefix + val.toFixed(1);
          else              el.textContent = prefix + Math.floor(val).toLocaleString('en-IN');
          if(prog<1) requestAnimationFrame(tick);
        };
        requestAnimationFrame(tick);
      });
    }

    function openModal(id)  { document.getElementById(id).classList.add('show'); }
    function closeModal(id) { document.getElementById(id).classList.remove('show'); }
    document.querySelectorAll('.modal-overlay').forEach(m => { m.addEventListener('click', e => { if(e.target===m) m.classList.remove('show'); }); });

    function showToast(icon, title, msg) {
      document.getElementById('toastIcon').textContent  = icon;
      document.getElementById('toastTitle').textContent = title;
      document.getElementById('toastMsg').textContent   = msg;
      const t = document.getElementById('toast');
      t.classList.add('show');
      setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), 3500);
    }

    function confirmDelete(what) {
      document.getElementById('deleteTarget').textContent = 'Are you sure you want to delete ' + what + '?';
      openModal('deleteModal');
    }

    function approveItem(type) { showToast('✅','Approved','The '+type+' has been approved and is now live.'); }

    function filterTable(q, tableId) {
      document.querySelectorAll('#'+tableId+' tbody tr').forEach(row => {
        row.style.display = row.textContent.toLowerCase().includes(q.toLowerCase()) ? '' : 'none';
      });
    }

    const sortDirs = {};
    function sortTable(tableId, col) {
      const key = tableId+col; sortDirs[key] = !sortDirs[key];
      const tbody = document.querySelector('#'+tableId+' tbody');
      if(!tbody) return;
      const rows = Array.from(tbody.querySelectorAll('tr'));
      rows.sort((a,b) => {
        const ta = a.cells[col]?.textContent.trim()||'';
        const tb = b.cells[col]?.textContent.trim()||'';
        const na = parseFloat(ta.replace(/[^0-9.]/g,''));
        const nb = parseFloat(tb.replace(/[^0-9.]/g,''));
        if(!isNaN(na)&&!isNaN(nb)) return sortDirs[key]?na-nb:nb-na;
        return sortDirs[key]?ta.localeCompare(tb):tb.localeCompare(ta);
      });
      rows.forEach(r => tbody.appendChild(r));
    }

    function selectAll(masterCb, tableId) {
      document.querySelectorAll('#'+tableId+' tbody input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(cb => { cb.checked = masterCb.checked; });
    }

    function exportData() { showToast('⬇','Export Started','Your CSV file is being prepared for download.'); }

    showTab('dashboard');
  </script>

</body>
</html>

  <script>
    // ── Reveal on scroll ──
    const reveals = document.querySelectorAll('.reveal');
    const io = new IntersectionObserver(entries => {
      entries.forEach(e => {
        if (e.isIntersecting) { e.target.classList.add('visible'); io.unobserve(e.target); }
      });
    }, { threshold: 0.08 });
    reveals.forEach(el => io.observe(el));

    // ── Star picker ──
    let selectedStars = 0;
    const labels = ['','Terrible 😞','Poor 😕','Okay 😐','Good 😊','Excellent 🤩'];
    function hoverStar(n) {
      document.querySelectorAll('.star-pick').forEach((s,i) => {
        s.classList.toggle('hovered', i < n);
      });
    }
    function unhoverStar() {
      document.querySelectorAll('.star-pick').forEach((s,i) => {
        s.classList.toggle('hovered', i < selectedStars);
      });
    }
    function selectStar(n) {
      selectedStars = n;
      document.querySelectorAll('.star-pick').forEach((s,i) => {
        s.classList.toggle('selected', i < n);
        s.classList.remove('hovered');
      });
      document.getElementById('ratingLabel').textContent = labels[n];
      document.getElementById('ratingLabel').style.color = '#a070d0';
    }

    // ── Tag chips ──
    function toggleTag(el) { el.classList.toggle('selected'); }

    // ── Char count ──
    function updateChar() {
      const val = document.getElementById('reviewText').value.length;
      document.getElementById('charCount').textContent = Math.min(val,500);
    }

    // ── Submit review ──
    function submitReview() {
      if (!selectedStars) { alert('Please select a star rating first!'); return; }
      const text = document.getElementById('reviewText').value.trim();
      if (text.length < 20) { alert('Please write at least 20 characters.'); return; }
      showToast('✅ Review submitted! It will appear after moderation.');
      selectedStars = 0;
      document.querySelectorAll('.star-pick').forEach(s => s.classList.remove('selected','hovered'));
      document.getElementById('ratingLabel').textContent = 'Click a star to rate';
      document.getElementById('ratingLabel').style.color = '';
      document.getElementById('reviewText').value = '';
      document.getElementById('charCount').textContent = '0';
      document.querySelectorAll('.tag-chip').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('selected'));
    }

    // ── Toast ──
    function showToast(msg) {
      const t = document.getElementById('toast');
      t.textContent = msg;
      t.classList.add('show');
      setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), 3000);
    }

    // ── Filter chips ──
    function setFilter(el, val) {
      document.querySelectorAll('.chip').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('active'));
      if (el) el.classList.add('active');
      const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.review-card');
      cards.forEach(card => {
        const stars = parseInt(card.dataset.stars);
        const hasPhotos = card.querySelector('.review-images');
        if (val === 'all') { card.style.display = ''; }
        else if (val === '5') { card.style.display = stars === 5 ? '' : 'none'; }
        else if (val === '4') { card.style.display = stars === 4 ? '' : 'none'; }
        else if (val === '3') { card.style.display = stars <= 3 ? '' : 'none'; }
        else if (val === 'photos') { card.style.display = hasPhotos ? '' : 'none'; }
      });
    }

    // ── Sort ──
    function sortReviews(val) {
      showToast(`✨ Sorted by: ${val}`);
    }

    // ── Helpful vote ──
    function vote(btn) {
      if (btn.classList.contains('voted')) return;
      btn.classList.add('voted');
      const span = btn.querySelector('.vote-count');
      span.textContent = parseInt(span.textContent) + 1;
    }

    // ── Event filter ──
    function filterByEvent(el) {
      document.querySelectorAll('.ef-item').forEach(i => i.classList.remove('active'));
      el.classList.add('active');
      showToast('🔍 Filtering reviews...');
    }
  </script>
</body>
</html>

    <h3>Reset Password</h3>

    <input type="email" id="fpEmail" placeholder="Email">
    <input type="password" id="newPass" placeholder="New Password">
    <input type="password" id="confirmPass" placeholder="Confirm Password">

<script>
// default admin
if(!localStorage.getItem("eventra_admin")){
  localStorage.setItem("eventra_admin", JSON.stringify({
    email:"admin@eventra.com",
    password:"admin123"
  }));
}

// toggle password
function togglePassword(){
  const p = document.getElementById("password");
  p.type = p.type === "password" ? "text" : "password";
}

// login
function login(e){
  e.preventDefault();

  const role = roleSelect();
  const emailVal = email.value;
  const passVal = password.value;
  const msg = document.getElementById("msg");

  if(role === "admin"){
    const admin = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("eventra_admin"));

    if(emailVal === admin.email && passVal === admin.password){
      localStorage.setItem("loggedIn","true");
      localStorage.setItem("role","admin");
      showMsg(msg,"Admin login successful",true);
      setTimeout(()=> window.location.href="admin.html",1000);
    } else {
      showMsg(msg,"Invalid admin credentials",false);
    }

  } else {
    const user = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("eventra_user"));

    if(!user){
      showMsg(msg,"No user found",false);
      return;
    }

    if(emailVal === user.email && passVal === user.password){
      localStorage.setItem("loggedIn","true");
      localStorage.setItem("role","user");
      showMsg(msg,"Login successful",true);
      setTimeout(()=> window.location.href="home.html",1000);
    } else {
      showMsg(msg,"Invalid user credentials",false);
    }
  }
}

function roleSelect(){
  return document.getElementById("role").value;
}

// messages
function showMsg(el,text,ok){
  el.textContent=text;
  el.className="message "+(ok?"success":"error");
}

// modal
function openModal(){
  document.getElementById("modal").style.display="flex";
}
function closeModal(){
  document.getElementById("modal").style.display="none";
}

// reset password
function resetPassword(){
  let user = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("eventra_user"));
  const msg = document.getElementById("fpMsg");

  if(!user){
    showMsg(msg,"No user found",false);
    return;
  }

  if(fpEmail.value !== user.email){
    showMsg(msg,"Email not found",false);
    return;
  }

  if(newPass.value !== confirmPass.value){
    showMsg(msg,"Passwords do not match",false);
    return;
  }

  user.password = newPass.value;
  localStorage.setItem("eventra_user", JSON.stringify(user));

  showMsg(msg,"Password updated!",true);
  setTimeout(closeModal,1000);
}
</script>

</body>
</html>

      <input type="text" id="name" placeholder="Full Name" required>
    </div>

      <input type="email" id="email" placeholder="Email" required>
    </div>

      <input type="password" id="password" placeholder="Password" required>

  </div>

<script>
function register(e){
  e.preventDefault();

  const user = {
    name: name.value,
    email: email.value,
    password: password.value
  };

  localStorage.setItem("eventra_user", JSON.stringify(user));

  alert("Account created!");
  window.location.href = "login.html";
}
</script>

  <script>
    /* ─── State persistence via sessionStorage ─── */
    const STATE_KEY = 'eventra_filter_state';

    function saveState() {
      const state = {
        search:   document.getElementById('searchInput').value,
        category: document.getElementById('categoryFilter').value,
        location: document.getElementById('locationFilter').value,
        date:     document.getElementById('dateFilter').value,
        sort:     document.getElementById('sortFilter').value,
        scrollY:  window.scrollY
      };
      sessionStorage.setItem(STATE_KEY, JSON.stringify(state));
    }

    function restoreState() {
      const raw = sessionStorage.getItem(STATE_KEY);
      if (!raw) return;
      try {
        const state = JSON.parse(raw);
        document.getElementById('searchInput').value    = state.search   || '';
        document.getElementById('categoryFilter').value = state.category || '';
        document.getElementById('locationFilter').value = state.location || '';
        document.getElementById('dateFilter').value     = state.date     || '';
        document.getElementById('sortFilter').value     = state.sort     || 'popular';
        filterEvents();
        if (state.scrollY) {
          requestAnimationFrame(() => window.scrollTo({ top: state.scrollY, behavior: 'instant' }));
        }
      } catch(e) {}
    }

    /* Save scroll position continuously */
    window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
      const raw = sessionStorage.getItem(STATE_KEY);
      if (raw) {
        try {
          const state = JSON.parse(raw);
          state.scrollY = window.scrollY;
          sessionStorage.setItem(STATE_KEY, JSON.stringify(state));
        } catch(e) {}
      }
    }, { passive: true });

    /* ─── Filter + Sort ─── */
    function filterEvents() {
      const q    = document.getElementById('searchInput').value.toLowerCase();
      const cat  = document.getElementById('categoryFilter').value;
      const loc  = document.getElementById('locationFilter').value;
      const dt   = document.getElementById('dateFilter').value;
      const sort = document.getElementById('sortFilter').value;

      const grid  = document.getElementById('eventsGrid');
      const cards = [...grid.querySelectorAll('.event-card')];

      let visible = cards.filter(c => {
        const match =
          (!q   || c.dataset.title.toLowerCase().includes(q)) &&
          (!cat || c.dataset.category === cat) &&
          (!loc || c.dataset.location  === loc) &&
          (!dt  || c.dataset.date      === dt);
        c.style.display = match ? '' : 'none';
        return match;
      });

      /* Sort visible cards */
      if (sort === 'price') {
        visible.sort((a, b) => parseInt(a.dataset.price) - parseInt(b.dataset.price));
      } else if (sort === 'newest') {
        const order = { march: 1, april: 2, may: 3 };
        visible.sort((a, b) => (order[a.dataset.date] || 9) - (order[b.dataset.date] || 9));
      } else {
        visible.sort((a, b) => parseInt(b.dataset.popularity) - parseInt(a.dataset.popularity));
      }

      /* Re-append in sorted order */
      visible.forEach(c => grid.appendChild(c));

      document.getElementById('resultCount').textContent = visible.length;

      let noRes = document.getElementById('noResults');
      if (visible.length === 0) {
        if (!noRes) {
          noRes = document.createElement('div');
          noRes.id = 'noResults'; noRes.className = 'no-results';
          noRes.innerHTML = '<div class="no-icon">🌸</div><p>No events match your filters — try adjusting them!</p>';
          grid.appendChild(noRes);
        }
      } else if (noRes) noRes.remove();
    }

    function resetFilters() {
      ['searchInput','categoryFilter','locationFilter','dateFilter'].forEach(id => {
        document.getElementById(id).value = '';
      });
      document.getElementById('sortFilter').value = 'popular';
      sessionStorage.removeItem(STATE_KEY);
      filterEvents();
    }

    /* ─── Modal ─── */
    let currentEvent = '';
    function openModal(name, date, location, price) {
      currentEvent = name;
      document.getElementById('modalEventName').textContent = name;
      document.getElementById('modalDate').textContent      = date;
      document.getElementById('modalLocation').textContent  = location;
      document.getElementById('modalPrice').textContent     = price;
      document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent     = 'Confirm Registration';
      document.getElementById('modalIcon').textContent      = '🎟';
      document.querySelector('.btn-confirm').style.display  = '';
      document.querySelector('.btn-close-modal').textContent = 'Cancel';
      document.getElementById('modal').querySelector('p').textContent = 'You\'re about to register for this event. Please confirm your spot below.';
      document.getElementById('modalOverlay').classList.add('open');
      document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
    }
    function closeModal() {
      document.getElementById('modalOverlay').classList.remove('open');
      document.body.style.overflow = '';
    }
    function handleOverlayClick(e) { if (e.target.id === 'modalOverlay') closeModal(); }
    function confirmRegistration() {
      document.getElementById('modalTitle').textContent     = 'You\'re Registered! 🎉';
      document.getElementById('modalIcon').textContent      = '✅';
      document.querySelector('.btn-confirm').style.display  = 'none';
      document.querySelector('.btn-close-modal').textContent = 'Close';
      document.getElementById('modal').querySelector('p').textContent = 'Your spot is confirmed. A confirmation email is on its way!';
      setTimeout(() => { closeModal(); showToast(currentEvent); }, 1800);
    }
    document.addEventListener('keydown', e => { if (e.key === 'Escape') closeModal(); });

    /* ─── Toast ─── */
    function showToast(event) {
      document.getElementById('toastTitle').textContent = 'Registered!';
      document.getElementById('toastMsg').textContent   = `Spot confirmed for "${event}"`;
      const t = document.getElementById('toast');
      t.classList.add('show');
      setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), 3800);
    }

    /* ─── Restore state on load ─── */
    restoreState();
  </script>
</body>
</html>
